WARNING:__main__:THIS TOOL IS OBSOLETE. The $NDK/toolchains/llvm/prebuilt/darwin-x86_64/bin directory contains
target-specific scripts that perform the same task. For example,
instead of:

    $ python $NDK/build/tools/make_standalone_toolchain.py \
        --arch arm --api 26 --install-dir toolchain
    $ toolchain/bin/clang++ src.cpp

Instead use:

    $ $NDK/toolchains/llvm/prebuilt/darwin-x86_64/bin/armv7a-linux-androideabi26-clang++ src.cpp

See https://developer.android.com/ndk/guides/other_build_systems for more
details.

WARNING:__main__:THIS TOOL IS OBSOLETE. The $NDK/toolchains/llvm/prebuilt/darwin-x86_64/bin directory contains
target-specific scripts that perform the same task. For example,
instead of:

    $ python $NDK/build/tools/make_standalone_toolchain.py \
        --arch x86 --api 26 --install-dir toolchain
    $ toolchain/bin/clang++ src.cpp

Instead use:

    $ $NDK/toolchains/llvm/prebuilt/darwin-x86_64/bin/i686-linux-android26-clang++ src.cpp

See https://developer.android.com/ndk/guides/other_build_systems for more
details.
